\DoxyCodeLine{314     \textcolor{comment}{// Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{315     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() = push window to the stack and start appending to it. End() = pop window from the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{316     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Passing 'bool* p\_open != NULL' shows a window-\/closing widget in the upper-\/right corner of the window,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{317     \textcolor{comment}{//   which clicking will set the boolean to false when clicked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{318     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may append multiple times to the same window during the same frame by calling Begin()/End() pairs multiple times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{319     \textcolor{comment}{//   Some information such as 'flags' or 'p\_open' will only be considered by the first call to Begin().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{320     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() return false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321     \textcolor{comment}{//   anything to the window. Always call a matching End() for each Begin() call, regardless of its return value!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note that the bottom of window stack always contains a window called "{}Debug"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          Begin(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* name, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{327     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          End();}
\DoxyCodeLine{328 }
\DoxyCodeLine{329     \textcolor{comment}{// Child Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use child windows to begin into a self-\/contained independent scrolling/clipping regions within a host window. Child windows can embed their own child.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For each independent axis of 'size': ==0.0f: use remaining host window size / >0.0f: fixed size / <0.0f: use remaining window size minus abs(size) / Each axis can use a different mode, e.g. ImVec2(0,400).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ BeginChild() returns false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting anything to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{333     \textcolor{comment}{//   Always call a matching EndChild() for each BeginChild() call, regardless of its return value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{334     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{335     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginChild(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0), \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} border = \textcolor{keyword}{false}, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{338     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginChild(ImGuiID \textcolor{keywordtype}{id}, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0), \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} border = \textcolor{keyword}{false}, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{424     \textcolor{comment}{// Cursor / Layout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{425     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ By "{}cursor"{} we mean the current output position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{426     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The typical widget behavior is to output themselves at the current cursor position, then move the cursor one line down.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{427     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can call SameLine() between widgets to undo the last carriage return and output at the right of the preceding widget.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{428     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Attention! We currently have inconsistencies between window-\/local and absolute positions we will aim to fix with future API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{429     \textcolor{comment}{//    Window-\/local coordinates:   SameLine(), GetCursorPos(), SetCursorPos(), GetCursorStartPos(), GetContentRegionMax(), GetWindowContentRegion*(), PushTextWrapPos()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{430     \textcolor{comment}{//    Absolute coordinate:        GetCursorScreenPos(), SetCursorScreenPos(), all ImDrawList:: functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{431     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          Separator();                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// separator, generally horizontal. inside a menu bar or in horizontal layout mode, this becomes a vertical separator.}}

X position given in window coordinates.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{455     \textcolor{comment}{// ID stack/scopes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{456     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the FAQ (docs/FAQ.md or http://dearimgui.org/faq) for more details about how ID are handled in dear imgui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{457     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those questions are answered and impacted by understanding of the ID stack system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{458     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: Why is my widget not reacting when I click on it?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{459     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have widgets with an empty label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{460     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have multiple widgets with the same label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{461     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Short version: ID are hashes of the entire ID stack. If you are creating widgets in a loop you most likely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{462     \textcolor{comment}{//   want to push a unique identifier (e.g. object pointer, loop index) to uniquely differentiate them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{463     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also use the "{}Label\#\#foobar"{} syntax within widget label to distinguish them from each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{464     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In this header file we use the "{}label"{}/"{}name"{} terminology to denote a string that will be displayed + used as an ID,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{465     \textcolor{comment}{//   whereas "{}str\_id"{} denote a string that is only used as an ID and not normally displayed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{466     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{467     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_begin, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_end);       \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{468     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* ptr\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push pointer into the ID stack (will hash pointer).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{469     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PushID(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} int\_id);                                             \textcolor{comment}{// push integer into the ID stack (will hash integer).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{470     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          PopID();                                                        \textcolor{comment}{// pop from the ID stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{471     IMGUI\_API ImGuiID       GetID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                      \textcolor{comment}{// calculate unique ID (hash of whole ID stack + given parameter). e.g. if you want to query into ImGuiStorage yourself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{472     IMGUI\_API ImGuiID       GetID(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_begin, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_end);}

\DoxyCodeLine{516     \textcolor{comment}{// Widgets: Drag Sliders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{517     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ CTRL+Click on any drag box to turn them into an input box. Manually input values aren't clamped by default and can go off-\/bounds. Use ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp to always clamp.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{518     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For all the Float2/Float3/Float4/Int2/Int3/Int4 versions of every functions, note that a 'float v[X]' function argument is the same as 'float* v',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{519     \textcolor{comment}{//   the array syntax is just a way to document the number of elements that are expected to be accessible. You can pass address of your first element out of a contiguous set, e.g. \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{520     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Adjust format string to decorate the value with a prefix, a suffix, or adapt the editing and display precision e.g. "{}\%.3f"{} -\/> 1.234; "{}\%5.2f secs"{} -\/> 01.23 secs; "{}Biscuit: \%.0f"{} -\/> Biscuit: 1; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{521     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Format string may also be set to NULL or use the default format ("{}\%f"{} or "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{522     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Speed are per-\/pixel of mouse movement (v\_speed=0.2f: mouse needs to move by 5 pixels to increase value by 1). For gamepad/keyboard navigation, minimum speed is Max(v\_speed, minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{523     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_min < v\_max to clamp edits to given limits. Note that CTRL+Click manual input can override those limits if ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{524     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_max = FLT\_MAX / INT\_MAX etc to avoid clamping to a maximum, same with v\_min = -\/FLT\_MAX / INT\_MIN to avoid clamping to a minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{525     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use the same sets of flags for DragXXX() and SliderXXX() functions as the features are the same and it makes it easier to swap them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{526     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Legacy: Pre-\/1.78 there are DragXXX() function signatures that takes a final `float power=1.0f' argument instead of the `ImGuiSliderFlags flags=0' argument.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{527     \textcolor{comment}{//   If you get a warning converting a float to ImGuiSliderFlags, read https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/3361}}
\DoxyCodeLine{528     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          DragFloat(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_speed = 1.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_min = 0.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_max = 0.0f, const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* format = "{}\%.3f"{}, ImGuiSliderFlags flags = 0);     \textcolor{comment}{// If v\_min >= v\_max we have no bound}}

\DoxyCodeLine{662     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups, Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{663     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They block normal mouse hovering detection (and therefore most mouse interactions) behind them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{664     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{665     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Their visibility state (\string~bool) is held internally instead of being held by the programmer as we are used to with regular Begin*() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{666     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The 3 properties above are related: we need to retain popup visibility state in the library because popups may be closed as any time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{667     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can bypass the hovering restriction by using ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup when calling IsItemHovered() or IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{668     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Popup identifiers are relative to the current ID stack, so OpenPopup and BeginPopup generally needs to be at the same level of the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{669     \textcolor{comment}{//    This is sometimes leading to confusing mistakes. May rework this in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{671     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: begin/end functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopup(): query popup state, if open start appending into the window. Call EndPopup() afterwards. ImGuiWindowFlags are forwarded to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopupModal(): block every interactions behind the window, cannot be closed by user, add a dimming background, has a title bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopup(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, ImGuiWindowFlags flags = 0);                         \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the popup is open, and you can start outputting to it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{676     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndPopup();                                                                         \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndPopup() if BeginPopupXXX() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677 }
\DoxyCodeLine{678     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: open/close functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ OpenPopup(): set popup state to open. ImGuiPopupFlags are available for opening options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{680     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup(): use inside the BeginPopup()/EndPopup() scope to close manually.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup() is called by default by Selectable()/MenuItem() when activated (FIXME: need some options).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Use ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup to avoid opening a popup if there's already one at the same level. This is equivalent to e.g. testing for !IsAnyPopupOpen() prior to OpenPopup().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Use IsWindowAppearing() after BeginPopup() to tell if a window just opened.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{685     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Notice that for OpenPopupOnItemClick() we exceptionally default flags to 1 (== ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight) for backward compatibility with older API taking 'int mouse\_button = 1' parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{686     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          OpenPopup(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, ImGuiPopupFlags popup\_flags = 0);                     \textcolor{comment}{// call to mark popup as open (don't call every frame!).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{691     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: open+begin combined functions helpers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Helpers to do OpenPopup+BeginPopup where the Open action is triggered by e.g. hovering an item and right-\/clicking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They are convenient to easily create context menus, hence the name.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{694     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Notice that BeginPopupContextXXX takes ImGuiPopupFlags just like OpenPopup() and unlike BeginPopup(). For full consistency, we may add ImGuiWindowFlags to the BeginPopupContextXXX functions in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Notice that we exceptionally default their flags to 1 (== ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight) for backward compatibility with older API taking 'int mouse\_button = 1' parameter, so if you add other flags remember to re-\/add the ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopupContextItem(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id = NULL, ImGuiPopupFlags popup\_flags = 1);  \textcolor{comment}{// open+begin popup when clicked on last item. Use str\_id==NULL to associate the popup to previous item. If you want to use that on a non-\/interactive item such as Text() you need to pass in an explicit ID here. read comments in .cpp!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopupContextWindow(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id = NULL, ImGuiPopupFlags popup\_flags = 1);\textcolor{comment}{// open+begin popup when clicked on current window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{698     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginPopupContextVoid(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id = NULL, ImGuiPopupFlags popup\_flags = 1);  \textcolor{comment}{// open+begin popup when clicked in void (where there are no windows).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{699 }
\DoxyCodeLine{700     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: query functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{701     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IsPopupOpen(): return true if the popup is open at the current BeginPopup() level of the popup stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{702     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IsPopupOpen() with ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId: return true if any popup is open at the current BeginPopup() level of the popup stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{703     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IsPopupOpen() with ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId + ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel: return true if any popup is open.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{704     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          IsPopupOpen(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, ImGuiPopupFlags flags = 0);                         \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the popup is open.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{706     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{707     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Full-\/featured replacement for old Columns API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{708     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See Demo-\/>Tables for demo code. See top of imgui\_tables.cpp for general commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{709     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See ImGuiTableFlags\_ and ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_ enums for a description of available flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{710     \textcolor{comment}{// The typical call flow is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{711     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 1. Call BeginTable(), early out if returning false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 2. Optionally call TableSetupColumn() to submit column name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 3. Optionally call TableSetupScrollFreeze() to request scroll freezing of columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 4. Optionally call TableHeadersRow() to submit a header row. Names are pulled from TableSetupColumn() data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Populate contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ In most situations you can use TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex(N) to start appending into a column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ If you are using tables as a sort of grid, where every columns is holding the same type of contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718     \textcolor{comment}{//      you may prefer using TableNextColumn() instead of TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{719     \textcolor{comment}{//      TableNextColumn() will automatically wrap-\/around into the next row if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ IMPORTANT: Comparatively to the old Columns() API, we need to call TableNextColumn() for the first column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Summary of possible call flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(0) -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(1) -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725     \textcolor{comment}{//                          TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK: TableNextColumn() automatically gets to next row!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{726     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow()                           -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{})                                               // Not OK! Missing TableSetColumnIndex() or TableNextColumn()! Text will not appear!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Call EndTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginTable(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column, ImGuiTableFlags flags = 0, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& outer\_size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0.0f, 0.0f), \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inner\_width = 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{730     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndTable();                                         \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndTable() if BeginTable() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{731     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableNextRow(ImGuiTableRowFlags row\_flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min\_row\_height = 0.0f); \textcolor{comment}{// append into the first cell of a new row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{732     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableNextColumn();                                  \textcolor{comment}{// append into the next column (or first column of next row if currently in last column). Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{733     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          TableSetColumnIndex(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n);                  \textcolor{comment}{// append into the specified column. Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{734 }
\DoxyCodeLine{735     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Headers \& Columns declaration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{736     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupColumn() to specify label, resizing policy, default width/weight, id, various other flags etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{737     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableHeadersRow() to create a header row and automatically submit a TableHeader() for each column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{738     \textcolor{comment}{//   Headers are required to perform: reordering, sorting, and opening the context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{739     \textcolor{comment}{//   The context menu can also be made available in columns body using ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{740     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may manually submit headers using TableNextRow() + TableHeader() calls, but this is only useful in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{741     \textcolor{comment}{//   some advanced use cases (e.g. adding custom widgets in header row).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{742     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupScrollFreeze() to lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{743     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableSetupColumn(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, ImGuiTableColumnFlags flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} init\_width\_or\_weight = 0.0f, ImGuiID user\_id = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{744     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableSetupScrollFreeze(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cols, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rows);         \textcolor{comment}{// lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{745     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableHeadersRow();                                  \textcolor{comment}{// submit all headers cells based on data provided to TableSetupColumn() + submit context menu}}
\DoxyCodeLine{746     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          TableHeader(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label);                     \textcolor{comment}{// submit one header cell manually (rarely used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{747 }
\DoxyCodeLine{748     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Sorting \& Miscellaneous functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{749     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Sorting: call TableGetSortSpecs() to retrieve latest sort specs for the table. NULL when not sorting.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{750     \textcolor{comment}{//   When 'sort\_specs-\/>SpecsDirty == true' you should sort your data. It will be true when sorting specs have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{751     \textcolor{comment}{//   changed since last call, or the first time. Make sure to set 'SpecsDirty = false' after sorting,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{752     \textcolor{comment}{//   else you may wastefully sort your data every frame!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{753     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Functions args 'int column\_n' treat the default value of -\/1 as the same as passing the current column index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{754     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_table_sort_specs}{ImGuiTableSortSpecs}}*  TableGetSortSpecs();                        \textcolor{comment}{// get latest sort specs for the table (NULL if not sorting).  Lifetime: don't hold on this pointer over multiple frames or past any subsequent call to BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{755     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetColumnCount();                      \textcolor{comment}{// return number of columns (value passed to BeginTable)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{756     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetColumnIndex();                      \textcolor{comment}{// return current column index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{757     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}                   TableGetRowIndex();                         \textcolor{comment}{// return current row index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{758     IMGUI\_API const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*           TableGetColumnName(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);      \textcolor{comment}{// return "{}"{} if column didn't have a name declared by TableSetupColumn(). Pass -\/1 to use current column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{759     IMGUI\_API ImGuiTableColumnFlags TableGetColumnFlags(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);     \textcolor{comment}{// return column flags so you can query their Enabled/Visible/Sorted/Hovered status flags. Pass -\/1 to use current column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{760     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}                  TableSetColumnEnabled(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} v);\textcolor{comment}{// change user accessible enabled/disabled state of a column. Set to false to hide the column. User can use the context menu to change this themselves (right-\/click in headers, or right-\/click in columns body with ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{761     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}                  TableSetBgColor(ImGuiTableBgTarget target, ImU32 color, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n = -\/1);  \textcolor{comment}{// change the color of a cell, row, or column. See ImGuiTableBgTarget\_ flags for details.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{792     \textcolor{comment}{// Drag and Drop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On source items, call BeginDragDropSource(), if it returns true also call SetDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropSource().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On target candidates, call BeginDragDropTarget(), if it returns true also call AcceptDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropTarget().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you stop calling BeginDragDropSource() the payload is preserved however it won't have a preview tooltip (we currently display a fallback "{}..."{} tooltip, see \#1725)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ An item can be both drag source and drop target.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          BeginDragDropSource(ImGuiDragDropFlags flags = 0);                                      \textcolor{comment}{// call after submitting an item which may be dragged. when this return true, you can call SetDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropSource()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          SetDragDropPayload(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* type, const \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} sz, ImGuiCond cond = 0);  \textcolor{comment}{// type is a user defined string of maximum 32 characters. Strings starting with '\_' are reserved for dear imgui internal types. Data is copied and held by imgui. Return true when payload has been accepted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{799     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          EndDragDropSource();                                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndDragDropSource() if BeginDragDropSource() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{800     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                  BeginDragDropTarget();                                                          \textcolor{comment}{// call after submitting an item that may receive a payload. If this returns true, you can call AcceptDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropTarget()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{801     IMGUI\_API const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_payload}{ImGuiPayload}}*   AcceptDragDropPayload(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* type, ImGuiDragDropFlags flags = 0);          \textcolor{comment}{// accept contents of a given type. If ImGuiDragDropFlags\_AcceptBeforeDelivery is set you can peek into the payload before the mouse button is released.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{802     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}                  EndDragDropTarget();                                                            \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndDragDropTarget() if BeginDragDropTarget() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{803     IMGUI\_API const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_payload}{ImGuiPayload}}*   GetDragDropPayload();                                                           \textcolor{comment}{// peek directly into the current payload from anywhere. may return NULL. use ImGuiPayload::IsDataType() to test for the payload type.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{807     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those can be nested but it cannot be used to enable an already disabled section (a single BeginDisabled(true) in the stack is enough to keep everything disabled)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{808     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ BeginDisabled(false) essentially does nothing useful but is provided to facilitate use of boolean expressions. If you can avoid calling BeginDisabled(False)/EndDisabled() best to avoid it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{941 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::Begin()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{942 enum ImGuiWindowFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{943 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{944     ImGuiWindowFlags\_None                   = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{945     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoTitleBar             = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable title-\/bar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{946     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoResize               = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user resizing with the lower-\/right grip}}
\DoxyCodeLine{947     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMove                 = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user moving the window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{948     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollbar            = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable scrollbars (window can still scroll with mouse or programmatically)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{949     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollWithMouse      = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user vertically scrolling with mouse wheel. On child window, mouse wheel will be forwarded to the parent unless NoScrollbar is also set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{950     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoCollapse             = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable user collapsing window by double-\/clicking on it. Also referred to as Window Menu Button (e.g. within a docking node).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{951     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize       = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Resize every window to its content every frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{952     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoBackground           = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable drawing background color (WindowBg, etc.) and outside border. Similar as using SetNextWindowBgAlpha(0.0f).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{953     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoSavedSettings        = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Never load/save settings in .ini file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{954     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMouseInputs          = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable catching mouse, hovering test with pass through.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{955     ImGuiWindowFlags\_MenuBar                = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Has a menu-\/bar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{956     ImGuiWindowFlags\_HorizontalScrollbar    = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow horizontal scrollbar to appear (off by default). You may use SetNextWindowContentSize(ImVec2(width,0.0f)); prior to calling Begin() to specify width. Read code in imgui\_demo in the "{}Horizontal Scrolling"{} section.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{957     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoFocusOnAppearing     = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable taking focus when transitioning from hidden to visible state}}
\DoxyCodeLine{958     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoBringToFrontOnFocus  = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable bringing window to front when taking focus (e.g. clicking on it or programmatically giving it focus)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{959     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysVerticalScrollbar= 1 << 14,  \textcolor{comment}{// Always show vertical scrollbar (even if ContentSize.y < Size.y)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{960     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysHorizontalScrollbar=1<< 15,  \textcolor{comment}{// Always show horizontal scrollbar (even if ContentSize.x < Size.x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{961     ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysUseWindowPadding = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Ensure child windows without border uses style.WindowPadding (ignored by default for non-\/bordered child windows, because more convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{962     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs            = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// No gamepad/keyboard navigation within the window}}
\DoxyCodeLine{963     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus             = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// No focusing toward this window with gamepad/keyboard navigation (e.g. skipped by CTRL+TAB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{964     ImGuiWindowFlags\_UnsavedDocument        = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Display a dot next to the title. When used in a tab/docking context, tab is selected when clicking the X + closure is not assumed (will wait for user to stop submitting the tab). Otherwise closure is assumed when pressing the X, so if you keep submitting the tab may reappear at end of tab bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{965     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNav                  = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus,}
\DoxyCodeLine{966     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoDecoration           = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoTitleBar | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoResize | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoScrollbar | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoCollapse,}
\DoxyCodeLine{967     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoInputs               = ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoMouseInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavInputs | ImGuiWindowFlags\_NoNavFocus,}
\DoxyCodeLine{968 }
\DoxyCodeLine{969     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{970     ImGuiWindowFlags\_NavFlattened           = 1 << 23,  \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] On child window: allow gamepad/keyboard navigation to cross over parent border to this child or between sibling child windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{971     ImGuiWindowFlags\_ChildWindow            = 1 << 24,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginChild()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{972     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Tooltip                = 1 << 25,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginTooltip()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{973     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Popup                  = 1 << 26,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginPopup()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{974     ImGuiWindowFlags\_Modal                  = 1 << 27,  \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginPopupModal()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{975     ImGuiWindowFlags\_ChildMenu              = 1 << 28   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't use! For internal use by BeginMenu()}}

\DoxyCodeLine{979 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::InputText()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{980 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiInputTextFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{981 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{982     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_None                = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{983     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CharsDecimal        = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Allow 0123456789.+-\/*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{984     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CharsHexadecimal    = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Allow 0123456789ABCDEFabcdef}}
\DoxyCodeLine{985     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CharsUppercase      = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Turn a..z into A..Z}}
\DoxyCodeLine{986     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CharsNoBlank        = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Filter out spaces, tabs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{987     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_AutoSelectAll       = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Select entire text when first taking mouse focus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{988     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_EnterReturnsTrue    = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Return 'true' when Enter is pressed (as opposed to every time the value was modified). Consider looking at the IsItemDeactivatedAfterEdit() function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{989     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCompletion  = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on pressing TAB (for completion handling)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{990     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackHistory     = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on pressing Up/Down arrows (for history handling)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{991     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackAlways      = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on each iteration. User code may query cursor position, modify text buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{992     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCharFilter  = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on character inputs to replace or discard them. Modify 'EventChar' to replace or discard, or return 1 in callback to discard.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{993     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_AllowTabInput       = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Pressing TAB input a '\(\backslash\)t' character into the text field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{994     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CtrlEnterForNewLine = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// In multi-\/line mode, unfocus with Enter, add new line with Ctrl+Enter (default is opposite: unfocus with Ctrl+Enter, add line with Enter).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{995     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_NoHorizontalScroll  = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable following the cursor horizontally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{996     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_AlwaysOverwrite     = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Overwrite mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{997     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_ReadOnly            = 1 << 14,  \textcolor{comment}{// Read-\/only mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{998     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_Password            = 1 << 15,  \textcolor{comment}{// Password mode, display all characters as '*'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{999     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_NoUndoRedo          = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable undo/redo. Note that input text owns the text data while active, if you want to provide your own undo/redo stack you need e.g. to call ClearActiveID().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1000     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CharsScientific     = 1 << 17,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow 0123456789.+-\/*/eE (Scientific notation input)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1001     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackResize      = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on buffer capacity changes request (beyond 'buf\_size' parameter value), allowing the string to grow. Notify when the string wants to be resized (for string types which hold a cache of their Size). You will be provided a new BufSize in the callback and NEED to honor it. (see misc/cpp/imgui\_stdlib.h for an example of using this)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1002     ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackEdit        = 1 << 19   \textcolor{comment}{// Callback on any edit (note that InputText() already returns true on edit, the callback is useful mainly to manipulate the underlying buffer while focus is active)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1003 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1004     \textcolor{comment}{// Obsolete names (will be removed soon)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1005 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1006     , ImGuiInputTextFlags\_AlwaysInsertMode    = ImGuiInputTextFlags\_AlwaysOverwrite   \textcolor{comment}{// [renamed in 1.82] name was not matching behavior}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1007 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1008 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1031 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1032 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(), IsPopupOpen() functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1033 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To be backward compatible with older API which took an 'int mouse\_button = 1' argument, we need to treat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1034 \textcolor{comment}{//   small flags values as a mouse button index, so we encode the mouse button in the first few bits of the flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1035 \textcolor{comment}{//   It is therefore guaranteed to be legal to pass a mouse button index in ImGuiPopupFlags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1036 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For the same reason, we exceptionally default the ImGuiPopupFlags argument of BeginPopupContextXXX functions to 1 instead of 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1037 \textcolor{comment}{//   IMPORTANT: because the default parameter is 1 (==ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight), if you rely on the default parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1038 \textcolor{comment}{//   and want to another another flag, you need to pass in the ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1039 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Multiple buttons currently cannot be combined/or-\/ed in those functions (we could allow it later).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1040 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiPopupFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1041 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1042     ImGuiPopupFlags\_None                    = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1043     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonLeft         = 0,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Left Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 0 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Left)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1044     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight        = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Right Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 1 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Right)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1045     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMiddle       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContext*(): open on Middle Mouse release. Guaranteed to always be == 2 (same as ImGuiMouseButton\_Middle)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1046     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonMask\_        = 0x1F,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1047     ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonDefault\_     = 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1048     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// For OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(): don't open if there's already a popup at the same level of the popup stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1049     ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverItems         = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// For BeginPopupContextWindow(): don't return true when hovering items, only when hovering empty space}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1050     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): ignore the ImGuiID parameter and test for any popup.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1051     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel           = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// For IsPopupOpen(): search/test at any level of the popup stack (default test in the current level)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1052     ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopup                = ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupId | ImGuiPopupFlags\_AnyPopupLevel}
\DoxyCodeLine{1053 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1054 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1110 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1111 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important! Sizing policies have complex and subtle side effects, much more so than you would expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1112 \textcolor{comment}{//   Read comments/demos carefully + experiment with live demos to get acquainted with them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1113 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DEFAULT sizing policies are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1114 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit    if ScrollX is on, or if host window has ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1115 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame if ScrollX is off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1116 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1117 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch with same weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1118 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Stretch (default), Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1119 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns (if any) will generally obtain their requested width (unless the table cannot fit them all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1120 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Stretch Columns will share the remaining width according to their respective weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1121 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Mixed Fixed/Stretch columns is possible but has various side-\/effects on resizing behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1122 \textcolor{comment}{//      The typical use of mixing sizing policies is: any number of LEADING Fixed columns, followed by one or two TRAILING Stretch columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1123 \textcolor{comment}{//      (this is because the visible order of columns have subtle but necessary effects on how they react to manual resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1124 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1125 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1126 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Fixed/Auto mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1127 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns can be enlarged as needed. Table will show an horizontal scrollbar if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1128 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ When using auto-\/resizing (non-\/resizable) fixed columns, querying the content width to use item right-\/alignment e.g. SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN) doesn't make sense, would create a feedback loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1129 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Using Stretch columns OFTEN DOES NOT MAKE SENSE if ScrollX is on, UNLESS you have specified a value for 'inner\_width' in BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1130 \textcolor{comment}{//      If you specify a value for 'inner\_width' then effectively the scrolling space is known and Stretch or mixed Fixed/Stretch columns become meaningful again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1131 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read on documentation at the top of imgui\_tables.cpp for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1132 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1133 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134     \textcolor{comment}{// Features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1135     ImGuiTableFlags\_None                       = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1136     ImGuiTableFlags\_Resizable                  = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable resizing columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137     ImGuiTableFlags\_Reorderable                = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable reordering columns in header row (need calling TableSetupColumn() + TableHeadersRow() to display headers)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1138     ImGuiTableFlags\_Hideable                   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable hiding/disabling columns in context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1139     ImGuiTableFlags\_Sortable                   = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable sorting. Call TableGetSortSpecs() to obtain sort specs. Also see ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti and ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1140     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoSavedSettings            = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Disable persisting columns order, width and sort settings in the .ini file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1141     ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody          = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Right-\/click on columns body/contents will display table context menu. By default it is available in TableHeadersRow().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1142     \textcolor{comment}{// Decorations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1143     ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg                      = 1 << 6,   \textcolor{comment}{// Set each RowBg color with ImGuiCol\_TableRowBg or ImGuiCol\_TableRowBgAlt (equivalent of calling TableSetBgColor with ImGuiTableBgFlags\_RowBg0 on each row manually)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1144     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH              = 1 << 7,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders between rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1145     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH              = 1 << 8,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders at the top and bottom.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1146     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV              = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders between columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1147     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV              = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders on the left and right sides.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1148     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersH                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw horizontal borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1149     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersV                   = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw vertical borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1150     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInnerH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw inner borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1151     ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter               = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterV | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuterH, \textcolor{comment}{// Draw outer borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1152     ImGuiTableFlags\_Borders                    = ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersInner | ImGuiTableFlags\_BordersOuter,   \textcolor{comment}{// Draw all borders.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1153     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBody            = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1154     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoBordersInBodyUntilResize = 1 << 12,  \textcolor{comment}{// [ALPHA] Disable vertical borders in columns Body until hovered for resize (borders will always appears in Headers). -\/> May move to style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1155     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Policy (read above for defaults)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1156     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit             = 1 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching contents width.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1157     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame            = 2 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthFixed or \_WidthAuto (if resizable or not resizable), matching the maximum contents width of all columns. Implicitly enable ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp          = 3 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights proportional to each columns contents widths.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame          = 4 << 13,  \textcolor{comment}{// Columns default to \_WidthStretch with default weights all equal, unless overridden by TableSetupColumn().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160     \textcolor{comment}{// Sizing Extra Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1161     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendX              = 1 << 16,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer width auto-\/fit to columns, overriding outer\_size.x value. Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled and Stretch columns are not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1162     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY              = 1 << 17,  \textcolor{comment}{// Make outer height stop exactly at outer\_size.y (prevent auto-\/extending table past the limit). Only available when ScrollX/ScrollY are disabled. Data below the limit will be clipped and not visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible       = 1 << 18,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable keeping column always minimally visible when ScrollX is off and table gets too small. Not recommended if columns are resizable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164     ImGuiTableFlags\_PreciseWidths              = 1 << 19,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable distributing remainder width to stretched columns (width allocation on a 100-\/wide table with 3 columns: Without this flag: 33,33,34. With this flag: 33,33,33). With larger number of columns, resizing will appear to be less smooth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165     \textcolor{comment}{// Clipping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoClip                     = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable clipping rectangle for every individual columns (reduce draw command count, items will be able to overflow into other columns). Generally incompatible with TableSetupScrollFreeze().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167     \textcolor{comment}{// Padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168     ImGuiTableFlags\_PadOuterX                  = 1 << 21,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is on. Enable outer-\/most padding. Generally desirable if you have headers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadOuterX                = 1 << 22,  \textcolor{comment}{// Default if BordersOuterV is off. Disable outer-\/most padding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170     ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadInnerX                = 1 << 23,  \textcolor{comment}{// Disable inner padding between columns (double inner padding if BordersOuterV is on, single inner padding if BordersOuterV is off).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171     \textcolor{comment}{// Scrolling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollX                    = 1 << 24,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable horizontal scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size. Changes default sizing policy. Because this create a child window, ScrollY is currently generally recommended when using ScrollX.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173     ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollY                    = 1 << 25,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable vertical scrolling. Require 'outer\_size' parameter of BeginTable() to specify the container size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174     \textcolor{comment}{// Sorting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortMulti                  = 1 << 26,  \textcolor{comment}{// Hold shift when clicking headers to sort on multiple column. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount > 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176     ImGuiTableFlags\_SortTristate               = 1 << 27,  \textcolor{comment}{// Allow no sorting, disable default sorting. TableGetSortSpecs() may return specs where (SpecsCount == 0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1178     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Combinations and masks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179     ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingMask\_                = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedSame | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp | ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1181     \textcolor{comment}{// Obsolete names (will be removed soon)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183     \textcolor{comment}{//, ImGuiTableFlags\_ColumnsWidthFixed = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit, ImGuiTableFlags\_ColumnsWidthStretch = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame   // WIP Tables 2020/12}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1184     \textcolor{comment}{//, ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingPolicyFixed = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit, ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingPolicyStretch = ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame   // WIP Tables 2021/01}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1185 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1237 \textcolor{comment}{// Enum for ImGui::TableSetBgColor()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1238 \textcolor{comment}{// Background colors are rendering in 3 layers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1239 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 0: draw with RowBg0 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg0 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1240 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 1: draw with RowBg1 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg1 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1241 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 2: draw with CellBg color if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1242 \textcolor{comment}{// The purpose of the two row/columns layers is to let you decide if a background color changes should override or blend with the existing color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1243 \textcolor{comment}{// When using ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg on the table, each row has the RowBg0 color automatically set for odd/even rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1244 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg0 target, your color will override the existing RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1245 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg1 or ColumnBg1 target, your color will blend over the RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1246 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiTableBgTarget\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1247 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1248     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_None                         = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1249     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg0                       = 1,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 0 (generally used for background, automatically set when ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg is used)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1250     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_RowBg1                       = 2,        \textcolor{comment}{// Set row background color 1 (generally used for selection marking)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1251     ImGuiTableBgTarget\_CellBg                       = 3         \textcolor{comment}{// Set cell background color (top-\/most color)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1252 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1253 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1426     \textcolor{comment}{// Keyboard Modifiers (explicitly submitted by backend via AddKeyEvent() calls)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1427     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is mirroring the data also written to io.KeyCtrl, io.KeyShift, io.KeyAlt, io.KeySuper, in a format allowing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1428     \textcolor{comment}{//   them to be accessed via standard key API, allowing calls such as IsKeyPressed(), IsKeyReleased(), querying duration etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1429     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Code polling every keys (e.g. an interface to detect a key press for input mapping) might want to ignore those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1430     \textcolor{comment}{//   and prefer using the real keys (e.g. ImGuiKey\_LeftCtrl, ImGuiKey\_RightCtrl instead of ImGuiKey\_ModCtrl).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1431     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In theory the value of keyboard modifiers should be roughly equivalent to a logical or of the equivalent left/right keys.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1432     \textcolor{comment}{//   In practice: it's complicated; mods are often provided from different sources. Keyboard layout, IME, sticky keys and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1433     \textcolor{comment}{//   backends tend to interfere and break that equivalence. The safer decision is to relay that ambiguity down to the end-\/user...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1434     ImGuiKey\_ModCtrl, ImGuiKey\_ModShift, ImGuiKey\_ModAlt, ImGuiKey\_ModSuper,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1435 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1436     \textcolor{comment}{// End of list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1437     ImGuiKey\_COUNT,                 \textcolor{comment}{// No valid ImGuiKey is ever greater than this value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1438 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1439     \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Prior to 1.87 we required user to fill io.KeysDown[512] using their own native index + a io.KeyMap[] array.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1440     \textcolor{comment}{// We are ditching this method but keeping a legacy path for user code doing e.g. IsKeyPressed(MY\_NATIVE\_KEY\_CODE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1441     ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_BEGIN         = 512,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1442     ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_END           = ImGuiKey\_COUNT,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1443     ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_COUNT         = ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_END -\/ ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_BEGIN,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1444 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_KEYIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1445     ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_SIZE          = ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_COUNT,          \textcolor{comment}{// Size of KeysData[]: only hold named keys}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1446     ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_OFFSET        = ImGuiKey\_NamedKey\_BEGIN           \textcolor{comment}{// First key stored in io.KeysData[0]. Accesses to io.KeysData[] must use (key -\/ ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_OFFSET).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1447 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1448     ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_SIZE          = ImGuiKey\_COUNT,                   \textcolor{comment}{// Size of KeysData[]: hold legacy 0..512 keycodes + named keys}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1449     ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_OFFSET        = 0                                 \textcolor{comment}{// First key stored in io.KeysData[0]. Accesses to io.KeysData[] must use (key -\/ ImGuiKey\_KeysData\_OFFSET).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1450 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1451 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1452 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1453     , ImGuiKey\_KeyPadEnter = ImGuiKey\_KeypadEnter   \textcolor{comment}{// Renamed in 1.87}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1454 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1455 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1467 \textcolor{comment}{// Gamepad/Keyboard navigation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1468 \textcolor{comment}{// Since >= 1.87 backends you generally don't need to care about this enum since io.NavInputs[] is setup automatically. This might become private/internal some day.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1469 \textcolor{comment}{// Keyboard: Set io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableKeyboard to enable. NewFrame() will automatically fill io.NavInputs[] based on your io.AddKeyEvent() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1470 \textcolor{comment}{// Gamepad:  Set io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableGamepad to enable. Backend: set ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasGamepad and fill the io.NavInputs[] fields before calling NewFrame(). Note that io.NavInputs[] is cleared by EndFrame().}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1501 \textcolor{comment}{// Configuration flags stored in io.ConfigFlags. Set by user/application.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1502 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImGuiConfigFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{1503 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1504     ImGuiConfigFlags\_None                   = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1505     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableKeyboard      = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Master keyboard navigation enable flag. NewFrame() will automatically fill io.NavInputs[] based on io.AddKeyEvent() calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1506     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableGamepad       = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Master gamepad navigation enable flag. This is mostly to instruct your imgui backend to fill io.NavInputs[]. Backend also needs to set ImGuiBackendFlags\_HasGamepad.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1507     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavEnableSetMousePos   = 1 << 2,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct navigation to move the mouse cursor. May be useful on TV/console systems where moving a virtual mouse is awkward. Will update io.MousePos and set io.WantSetMousePos=true. If enabled you MUST honor io.WantSetMousePos requests in your backend, otherwise ImGui will react as if the mouse is jumping around back and forth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1508     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NavNoCaptureKeyboard   = 1 << 3,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct navigation to not set the io.WantCaptureKeyboard flag when io.NavActive is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1509     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NoMouse                = 1 << 4,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct imgui to clear mouse position/buttons in NewFrame(). This allows ignoring the mouse information set by the backend.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1510     ImGuiConfigFlags\_NoMouseCursorChange    = 1 << 5,   \textcolor{comment}{// Instruct backend to not alter mouse cursor shape and visibility. Use if the backend cursor changes are interfering with yours and you don't want to use SetMouseCursor() to change mouse cursor. You may want to honor requests from imgui by reading GetMouseCursor() yourself instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1512     \textcolor{comment}{// User storage (to allow your backend/engine to communicate to code that may be shared between multiple projects. Those flags are NOT used by core Dear ImGui)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1513     ImGuiConfigFlags\_IsSRGB                 = 1 << 20,  \textcolor{comment}{// Application is SRGB-\/aware.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1514     ImGuiConfigFlags\_IsTouchScreen          = 1 << 21   \textcolor{comment}{// Application is using a touch screen instead of a mouse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1515 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1516 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1742 \textcolor{comment}{// IM\_MALLOC(), IM\_FREE(), IM\_NEW(), IM\_PLACEMENT\_NEW(), IM\_DELETE()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1743 \textcolor{comment}{// We call C++ constructor on own allocated memory via the placement "{}new(ptr) Type()"{} syntax.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1744 \textcolor{comment}{// Defining a custom placement new() with a custom parameter allows us to bypass including <new> which on some platforms complains when user has disabled exceptions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1745 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1757 \textcolor{comment}{// ImVector<>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1758 \textcolor{comment}{// Lightweight std::vector<>-\/like class to avoid dragging dependencies (also, some implementations of STL with debug enabled are absurdly slow, we bypass it so our code runs fast in debug).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1759 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1760 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You generally do NOT need to care or use this ever. But we need to make it available in imgui.h because some of our public structures are relying on it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1761 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use std-\/like naming convention here, which is a little unusual for this codebase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1762 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: clear() frees memory, resize(0) keep the allocated buffer. We use resize(0) a lot to intentionally recycle allocated buffers across frames and amortize our costs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1763 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: our implementation does NOT call C++ constructors/destructors, we treat everything as raw data! This is intentional but be extra mindful of that,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1764 \textcolor{comment}{//   Do NOT use this class as a std::vector replacement in your own code! Many of the structures used by dear imgui can be safely initialized by a zero-\/memset.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1765 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1766 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1767 IM\_MSVC\_RUNTIME\_CHECKS\_OFF}

\DoxyCodeLine{1806     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         swap(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<T>}}\& rhs)              \{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rhs\_size = rhs.Size; rhs.Size = Size; Size = rhs\_size; \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rhs\_cap = rhs.Capacity; rhs.Capacity = Capacity; Capacity = rhs\_cap; T* rhs\_data = rhs.Data; rhs.Data = Data; Data = rhs\_data; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1808     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}          \_grow\_capacity(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sz)\textcolor{keyword}{ const        }\{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_capacity = Capacity ? (Capacity + Capacity / 2) : 8; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} new\_capacity > sz ? new\_capacity : sz; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         resize(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_size)                \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (new\_size > Capacity) reserve(\_grow\_capacity(new\_size)); Size = new\_size; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         resize(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_size, \textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)    \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (new\_size > Capacity) reserve(\_grow\_capacity(new\_size)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (new\_size > Size) \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} n = Size; n < new\_size; n++) memcpy(\&Data[n], \&v, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(v)); Size = new\_size; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         shrink(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_size)                \{ IM\_ASSERT(new\_size <= Size); Size = new\_size; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Resize a vector to a smaller size, guaranteed not to cause a reallocation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         reserve(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_capacity)           \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (new\_capacity <= Capacity) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}; T* new\_data = (T*)IM\_ALLOC((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})new\_capacity * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (Data) \{ memcpy(new\_data, Data, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})Size * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); IM\_FREE(Data); \} Data = new\_data; Capacity = new\_capacity; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         reserve\_discard(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} new\_capacity)   \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (new\_capacity <= Capacity) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (Data) IM\_FREE(Data); Data = (T*)IM\_ALLOC((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})new\_capacity * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); Capacity = new\_capacity; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1815     \textcolor{comment}{// NB: It is illegal to call push\_back/push\_front/insert with a reference pointing inside the ImVector data itself! e.g. v.push\_back(v[10]) is forbidden.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         push\_back(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)               \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (Size == Capacity) reserve(\_grow\_capacity(Size + 1)); memcpy(\&Data[Size], \&v, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(v)); Size++; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         pop\_back()                          \{ IM\_ASSERT(Size > 0); Size-\/-\/; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}         push\_front(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)              \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (Size == 0) push\_back(v); \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} insert(Data, v); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} T*           erase(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it)                  \{ IM\_ASSERT(it >= Data \&\& it < Data + Size); \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t off = it -\/ Data; memmove(Data + off, Data + off + 1, ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})Size -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})off -\/ 1) * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); Size-\/-\/; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Data + off; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} T*           erase(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it, \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it\_last)\{ IM\_ASSERT(it >= Data \&\& it < Data + Size \&\& it\_last >= it \&\& it\_last <= Data + Size); \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t count = it\_last -\/ it; \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t off = it -\/ Data; memmove(Data + off, Data + off + count, ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})Size -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})off -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})count) * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); Size -\/= (int)count; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Data + off; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} T*           erase\_unsorted(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it)         \{ IM\_ASSERT(it >= Data \&\& it < Data + Size);  \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t off = it -\/ Data; \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (it < Data + Size -\/ 1) memcpy(Data + off, Data + Size -\/ 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); Size-\/-\/; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Data + off; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} T*           insert(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it, \textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)     \{ IM\_ASSERT(it >= Data \&\& it <= Data + Size); \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t off = it -\/ Data; \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (Size == Capacity) reserve(\_grow\_capacity(Size + 1)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (off < (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})Size) memmove(Data + off + 1, Data + off, ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})Size -\/ (\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})off) * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T)); memcpy(\&Data[off], \&v, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(v)); Size++; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Data + off; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}         contains(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)\textcolor{keyword}{ const          }\{ \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* data = Data;  \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* data\_end = Data + Size; \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (data < data\_end) \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*data++ == v) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false}; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} T*           find(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)                    \{ T* data = Data;  \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* data\_end = Data + Size; \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (data < data\_end) \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*data == v) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} ++data; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} data; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1825     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keyword}{const} T*     find(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)\textcolor{keyword}{ const              }\{ \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* data = Data;  \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* data\_end = Data + Size; \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (data < data\_end) \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*data == v) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} ++data; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} data; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}         find\_erase(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)              \{ \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it = find(v); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (it < Data + Size) \{ erase(it); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true}; \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false}; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}         find\_erase\_unsorted(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T\& v)     \{ \textcolor{keyword}{const} T* it = find(v); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (it < Data + Size) \{ erase\_unsorted(it); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true}; \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false}; \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2068 \textcolor{comment}{// The callback function should return 0 by default.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069 \textcolor{comment}{// Callbacks (follow a flag name and see comments in ImGuiInputTextFlags\_ declarations for more details)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackEdit:        Callback on buffer edit (note that InputText() already returns true on edit, the callback is useful mainly to manipulate the underlying buffer while focus is active)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackAlways:      Callback on each iteration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCompletion:  Callback on pressing TAB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackHistory:     Callback on pressing Up/Down arrows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackCharFilter:  Callback on character inputs to replace or discard them. Modify 'EventChar' to replace or discard, or return 1 in callback to discard.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ ImGuiInputTextFlags\_CallbackResize:      Callback on buffer capacity changes request (beyond 'buf\_size' parameter value), allowing the string to grow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_input_text_callback_data}{ImGuiInputTextCallbackData}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2229 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Key-\/>Value storage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2230 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically you don't have to worry about this since a storage is held within each Window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231 \textcolor{comment}{// We use it to e.g. store collapse state for a tree (Int 0/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2232 \textcolor{comment}{// This is optimized for efficient lookup (dichotomy into a contiguous buffer) and rare insertion (typically tied to user interactions aka max once a frame)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2233 \textcolor{comment}{// You can use it as custom user storage for temporary values. Declare your own storage if, for example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to manipulate the open/close state of a particular sub-\/tree in your interface (tree node uses Int 0/1 to store their state).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2235 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to store custom debug data easily without adding or editing structures in your code (probably not efficient, but convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236 \textcolor{comment}{// Types are NOT stored, so it is up to you to make sure your Key don't collide with different types.}}
