\DoxyCodeLine{2279 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2280 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Manually clip large list of items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2281 \textcolor{comment}{// If you have lots evenly spaced items and you have a random access to the list, you can perform coarse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2282 \textcolor{comment}{// clipping based on visibility to only submit items that are in view.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2283 \textcolor{comment}{// The clipper calculates the range of visible items and advance the cursor to compensate for the non-\/visible items we have skipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2284 \textcolor{comment}{// (Dear ImGui already clip items based on their bounds but: it needs to first layout the item to do so, and generally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2285 \textcolor{comment}{//  fetching/submitting your own data incurs additional cost. Coarse clipping using ImGuiListClipper allows you to easily}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2286 \textcolor{comment}{//  scale using lists with tens of thousands of items without a problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2287 \textcolor{comment}{// Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2288 \textcolor{comment}{//   ImGuiListClipper clipper;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2289 \textcolor{comment}{//   clipper.Begin(1000);         // We have 1000 elements, evenly spaced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2290 \textcolor{comment}{//   while (clipper.Step())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2291 \textcolor{comment}{//       for (int i = clipper.DisplayStart; i < clipper.DisplayEnd; i++)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2292 \textcolor{comment}{//           ImGui::Text("{}line number \%d"{}, i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2293 \textcolor{comment}{// Generally what happens is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2294 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper lets you process the first element (DisplayStart = 0, DisplayEnd = 1) regardless of it being visible or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2295 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit that one element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2296 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper can measure the height of the first element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2297 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper calculate the actual range of elements to display based on the current clipping rectangle, position the cursor before the first visible element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2298 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit visible elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2299 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The clipper also handles various subtleties related to keyboard/gamepad navigation, wrapping etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2300 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2301 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2302     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             DisplayStart;       \textcolor{comment}{// First item to display, updated by each call to Step()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2303     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             DisplayEnd;         \textcolor{comment}{// End of items to display (exclusive)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2304     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             ItemsCount;         \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Number of items}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2305     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}           ItemsHeight;        \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Height of item after a first step and item submission can calculate it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2306     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}           StartPosY;          \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Cursor position at the time of Begin() or after table frozen rows are all processed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2307     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*           TempData;           \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Internal data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2308 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2309     \textcolor{comment}{// items\_count: Use INT\_MAX if you don't know how many items you have (in which case the cursor won't be advanced in the final step)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2310     \textcolor{comment}{// items\_height: Use -\/1.0f to be calculated automatically on first step. Otherwise pass in the distance between your items, typically GetTextLineHeightWithSpacing() or GetFrameHeightWithSpacing().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2311     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2312     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{\string~ImGuiListClipper}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2313     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}  Begin(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} items\_count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} items\_height = -\/1.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2314     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}  End();             \textcolor{comment}{// Automatically called on the last call of Step() that returns false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2315     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}  Step();            \textcolor{comment}{// Call until it returns false. The DisplayStart/DisplayEnd fields will be set and you can process/draw those items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2316 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2317     \textcolor{comment}{// Call ForceDisplayRangeByIndices() before first call to Step() if you need a range of items to be displayed regardless of visibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2318     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}  ForceDisplayRangeByIndices(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} item\_min, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} item\_max); \textcolor{comment}{// item\_max is exclusive e.g. use (42, 42+1) to make item 42 always visible BUT due to alignment/padding of certain items it is likely that an extra item may be included on either end of the display range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2319 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2320 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IMGUI\_DISABLE\_OBSOLETE\_FUNCTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2321     \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} items\_count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} items\_height = -\/1.0f) \{ memset(\textcolor{keyword}{this}, 0, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(*\textcolor{keyword}{this})); ItemsCount = -\/1; Begin(items\_count, items\_height); \} \textcolor{comment}{// [removed in 1.79]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2322 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2323 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{2378 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawCallback: Draw callbacks for advanced uses [configurable type: override in imconfig.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2379 \textcolor{comment}{// NB: You most likely do NOT need to use draw callbacks just to create your own widget or customized UI rendering,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2380 \textcolor{comment}{// you can poke into the draw list for that! Draw callback may be useful for example to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2381 \textcolor{comment}{//  A) Change your GPU render state,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2382 \textcolor{comment}{//  B) render a complex 3D scene inside a UI element without an intermediate texture/render target, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2383 \textcolor{comment}{// The expected behavior from your rendering function is 'if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL) \{ cmd.UserCallback(parent\_list, cmd); \} else \{ RenderTriangles() \}'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2384 \textcolor{comment}{// If you want to override the signature of ImDrawCallback, you can simply use e.g. '\#define ImDrawCallback MyDrawCallback' (in imconfig.h) + update rendering backend accordingly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2385 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef ImDrawCallback}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2386 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} void (*ImDrawCallback)(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_list}{ImDrawList}}* parent\_list, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_draw_cmd}{ImDrawCmd}}* cmd);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2387 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2388 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2389 \textcolor{comment}{// Special Draw callback value to request renderer backend to reset the graphics/render state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2390 \textcolor{comment}{// The renderer backend needs to handle this special value, otherwise it will crash trying to call a function at this address.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2391 \textcolor{comment}{// This is useful for example if you submitted callbacks which you know have altered the render state and you want it to be restored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2392 \textcolor{comment}{// It is not done by default because they are many perfectly useful way of altering render state for imgui contents (e.g. changing shader/blending settings before an Image call).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2393 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ImDrawCallback\_ResetRenderState     (ImDrawCallback)(-\/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2394 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2395 \textcolor{comment}{// Typically, 1 command = 1 GPU draw call (unless command is a callback)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2396 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ VtxOffset: When 'io.BackendFlags \& ImGuiBackendFlags\_RendererHasVtxOffset' is enabled,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2397 \textcolor{comment}{//   this fields allow us to render meshes larger than 64K vertices while keeping 16-\/bit indices.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2398 \textcolor{comment}{//   Backends made for <1.71. will typically ignore the VtxOffset fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2399 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The ClipRect/TextureId/VtxOffset fields must be contiguous as we memcmp() them together (this is asserted for).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2426 \textcolor{comment}{// The code expect ImVec2 pos (8 bytes), ImVec2 uv (8 bytes), ImU32 col (4 bytes), but you can re-\/order them or add other fields as needed to simplify integration in your engine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427 \textcolor{comment}{// The type has to be described within the macro (you can either declare the struct or use a typedef). This is because ImVec2/ImU32 are likely not declared a the time you'd want to set your type up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: IMGUI DOESN'T CLEAR THE STRUCTURE AND DOESN'T CALL A CONSTRUCTOR SO ANY CUSTOM FIELD WILL BE UNINITIALIZED. IF YOU ADD EXTRA FIELDS (SUCH AS A 'Z' COORDINATES) YOU WILL NEED TO CLEAR THEM DURING RENDER OR TO IGNORE THEM.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2448 \textcolor{comment}{// Split/Merge functions are used to split the draw list into different layers which can be drawn into out of order.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2465 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImDrawList functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466 \textcolor{comment}{// (Legacy: bit 0 must always correspond to ImDrawFlags\_Closed to be backward compatible with old API using a bool. Bits 1..3 must be unused)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImDrawFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2469     ImDrawFlags\_None                        = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2470     ImDrawFlags\_Closed                      = 1 << 0, \textcolor{comment}{// PathStroke(), AddPolyline(): specify that shape should be closed (Important: this is always == 1 for legacy reason)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2471     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft         = 1 << 4, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x01.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2472     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight        = 1 << 5, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding top-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x02.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2473     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft      = 1 << 6, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/left corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Was 0x04.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2474     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight     = 1 << 7, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): enable rounding bottom-\/right corner only (when rounding > 0.0f, we default to all corners). Wax 0x08.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone            = 1 << 8, \textcolor{comment}{// AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect(): disable rounding on all corners (when rounding > 0.0f). This is NOT zero, NOT an implicit flag!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTop             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottom          = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersLeft            = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersRight           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll             = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersTopRight | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomLeft | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersBottomRight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersDefault\_        = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll, \textcolor{comment}{// Default to ALL corners if none of the \_RoundCornersXX flags are specified.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2482     ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersMask\_           = ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersAll | ImDrawFlags\_RoundCornersNone}
\DoxyCodeLine{2483 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{2489     ImDrawListFlags\_None                    = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2490     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedLines        = 1 << 0,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased lines/borders (*2 the number of triangles for 1.0f wide line or lines thin enough to be drawn using textures, otherwise *3 the number of triangles)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2491     ImDrawListFlags\_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex  = 1 << 1,  \textcolor{comment}{// Enable anti-\/aliased lines/borders using textures when possible. Require backend to render with bilinear filtering (NOT point/nearest filtering).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2496 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw command list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2497 \textcolor{comment}{// This is the low-\/level list of polygons that ImGui:: functions are filling. At the end of the frame,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2498 \textcolor{comment}{// all command lists are passed to your ImGuiIO::RenderDrawListFn function for rendering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499 \textcolor{comment}{// Each dear imgui window contains its own ImDrawList. You can use ImGui::GetWindowDrawList() to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500 \textcolor{comment}{// access the current window draw list and draw custom primitives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2501 \textcolor{comment}{// You can interleave normal ImGui:: calls and adding primitives to the current draw list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2502 \textcolor{comment}{// In single viewport mode, top-\/left is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos (generally 0,0), bottom-\/right is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos+Size (generally io.DisplaySize).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2503 \textcolor{comment}{// You are totally free to apply whatever transformation matrix to want to the data (depending on the use of the transformation you may want to apply it to ClipRect as well!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2504 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: Primitives are always added to the list and not culled (culling is done at higher-\/level by ImGui:: functions), if you use this API a lot consider coarse culling your drawn objects.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2718     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font}{ImFont}}*         Font;           \textcolor{comment}{// Input    // For custom font glyphs only: target font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas_custom_rect}{ImFontAtlasCustomRect}}()         \{ Width = Height = 0; X = Y = 0xFFFF; GlyphID = 0; GlyphAdvanceX = 0.0f; GlyphOffset = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0); Font = NULL; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} IsPacked()\textcolor{keyword}{ const           }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} X != 0xFFFF; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImFontAtlas build}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} ImFontAtlasFlags\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726     ImFontAtlasFlags\_None               = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoPowerOfTwoHeight = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't round the height to next power of two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors     = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build software mouse cursors into the atlas (save a little texture memory)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729     ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoBakedLines       = 1 << 2    \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build thick line textures into the atlas (save a little texture memory, allow support for point/nearest filtering). The AntiAliasedLinesUseTex features uses them, otherwise they will be rendered using polygons (more expensive for CPU/GPU).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{comment}{// Load and rasterize multiple TTF/OTF fonts into a same texture. The font atlas will build a single texture holding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ One or more fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Custom graphics data needed to render the shapes needed by Dear ImGui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Mouse cursor shapes for software cursor rendering (unless setting 'Flags |= ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors' in the font atlas).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{// It is the user-\/code responsibility to setup/build the atlas, then upload the pixel data into a texture accessible by your graphics api.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Optionally, call any of the AddFont*** functions. If you don't call any, the default font embedded in the code will be loaded for you.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call GetTexDataAsAlpha8() or GetTexDataAsRGBA32() to build and retrieve pixels data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Upload the pixels data into a texture within your graphics system (see imgui\_impl\_xxxx.cpp examples)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call SetTexID(my\_tex\_id); and pass the pointer/identifier to your texture in a format natural to your graphics API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{comment}{//    This value will be passed back to you during rendering to identify the texture. Read FAQ entry about ImTextureID for more details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 \textcolor{comment}{// Common pitfalls:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you pass a 'glyph\_ranges' array to AddFont*** functions, you need to make sure that your array persist up until the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{comment}{//   atlas is build (when calling GetTexData*** or Build()). We only copy the pointer, not the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: By default, AddFontFromMemoryTTF() takes ownership of the data. Even though we are not writing to it, we will free the pointer on destruction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 \textcolor{comment}{//   You can set font\_cfg-\/>FontDataOwnedByAtlas=false to keep ownership of your data and it won't be freed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Even though many functions are suffixed with "{}TTF"{}, OTF data is supported just as well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is an old API and it is currently awkward for those and and various other reasons! We will address them in the future!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{ImFontAtlas}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2750 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2751     IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{ImFontAtlas}}();}

\DoxyCodeLine{2764     \textcolor{comment}{// Build atlas, retrieve pixel data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2765     \textcolor{comment}{// User is in charge of copying the pixels into graphics memory (e.g. create a texture with your engine). Then store your texture handle with SetTexID().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2766     \textcolor{comment}{// The pitch is always = Width * BytesPerPixels (1 or 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2767     \textcolor{comment}{// Building in RGBA32 format is provided for convenience and compatibility, but note that unless you manually manipulate or copy color data into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2768     \textcolor{comment}{// the texture (e.g. when using the AddCustomRect*** api), then the RGB pixels emitted will always be white (\string~75\% of memory/bandwidth waste.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2769     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}              Build();                    \textcolor{comment}{// Build pixels data. This is called automatically for you by the GetTexData*** functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2770     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              GetTexDataAsAlpha8(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}** out\_pixels, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_bytes\_per\_pixel = NULL);  \textcolor{comment}{// 1 byte per-\/pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2771     IMGUI\_API \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}              GetTexDataAsRGBA32(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}** out\_pixels, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}* out\_bytes\_per\_pixel = NULL);  \textcolor{comment}{// 4 bytes-\/per-\/pixel}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2795     \textcolor{comment}{// You can request arbitrary rectangles to be packed into the atlas, for your own purposes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2796     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ After calling Build(), you can query the rectangle position and render your pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2797     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you render colored output, set 'atlas-\/>TexPixelsUseColors = true' as this may help some backends decide of prefered texture format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2798     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also request your rectangles to be mapped as font glyph (given a font + Unicode point),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2799     \textcolor{comment}{//   so you can render e.g. custom colorful icons and use them as regular glyphs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2800     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read docs/FONTS.md for more details about using colorful icons.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2913 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2914 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Currently represents the Platform Window created by the application which is hosting our Dear ImGui windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In 'docking' branch with multi-\/viewport enabled, we extend this concept to have multiple active viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In the future we will extend this concept further to also represent Platform Monitor and support a "{}no main platform window"{} operation mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2917 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ About Main Area vs Work Area:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2918 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Main Area = entire viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Work Area = entire viewport minus sections used by main menu bars (for platform windows), or by task bar (for platform monitor).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2920 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Windows are generally trying to stay within the Work Area of their host viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2921 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2925     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              Size;                   \textcolor{comment}{// Main Area: Size of the viewport.}}
